<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-f4fc0af" data-v="4" data-block-id="f4fc0af"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-f4fc0af-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-f4fc0af-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-140a48e" data-block-id="140a48e"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk--block-align-140a48e stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-140a48e-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-933527c" data-v="4" data-block-id="933527c"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-933527c-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-933527c-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-15bfd05" id="our-story" data-block-id="15bfd05"><h1 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-center">Curriculum</h1></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-9167e55 stk-entrance stk-will-enter stk-entered stk-entrance-done" id="our-story" data-block-id="9167e55"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-align-center">Learning through Play and Exploration</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-image stk-block-image stk-block stk-9901b85 stk-entrance wp-mfs-content-banner stk-will-enter stk-entered stk-entrance-done" data-block-id="9901b85"><figure class="stk-img-wrapper stk-image--shape-stretch"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" class="stk-img wp-image-9773" src="https://www.myfirstskool.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/banner-curriculum.jpg" width="1920" height="672"></figure></div>
</div></div></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-24e28e2" data-block-id="24e28e2"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-24e28e2-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-f318cc5" data-v="4" data-block-id="f318cc5"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-f318cc5-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-f318cc5-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading alignfull stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-26d6d4e" id="relationships-the-heart-of-our-curriculum" data-block-id="26d6d4e"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Relationships: the heart of our curriculum</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-a26d157" data-block-id="a26d157"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">With over 40 years of expertise in child development, My First Skool ensures that our curriculum stays current with the latest developments in early childhood to equip children at that stage in their development with the right skills and mindset to thrive in this ever-changing world.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-49b56f6" data-block-id="49b56f6"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">We recognise that children are unique individuals. They explore their environment, form opinions, and want to be heard. As such, we centre our curriculum around relationships, forging close bonds, and building genuine connections with the children and parents.

</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-b530842" data-block-id="b530842"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">Children who receive encouragement and love are more eager to learn and play; and are empowered with the social competency skills needed to navigate different situations.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-71c6eb2" data-block-id="71c6eb2"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-71c6eb2-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-c7e2f0f stk-entrance stk-will-enter" data-v="4" data-block-id="c7e2f0f"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-c7e2f0f-container stk-hover-parent"><div class="has-text-align-center stk--column-flex stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-c7e2f0f-inner-blocks stk--align-last-block-to-bottom">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-7bb065e" id="infant-to-nursery-1" data-block-id="7bb065e"><h3 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">Infant to Nursery 1</h3></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-8b4accb" id="2-months-to-3-years-old" data-block-id="8b4accb"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">2 months to 3 years old</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-bc84434" data-block-id="bc84434"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">Adopting a Relationships-based Approach to Early Years Education</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-button-group stk-block-button-group stk-block stk-e8dd078" id="title-for-this-block" data-block-id="e8dd078"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks has-text-align-left stk-block-content stk-button-group">

</div></div>
</div><a class="stk-link stk-block-link stk--transparent-overlay" href="https://www.myfirstskool.com/curriculum/infant-to-nursery-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-695e476 stk-entrance stk-will-enter" data-v="4" data-block-id="695e476"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-695e476-container stk-hover-parent"><div class="has-text-align-center stk--column-flex stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-695e476-inner-blocks stk--align-last-block-to-bottom">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-5af57ea" id="nursery-2-to-kindergarten-2" data-block-id="5af57ea"><h3 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">Nursery 2 to Kindergarten 2</h3></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-132c698" id="4-to-6-years-old" data-block-id="132c698"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">4 to 6 years old</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-a4fd75c" data-block-id="a4fd75c"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">Adopting a Relationships-based Approach to Primary Education &amp; Society</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-button-group stk-block-button-group stk-block stk-82702d9" id="title-for-this-block" data-block-id="82702d9"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks has-text-align-left stk-block-content stk-button-group">

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-6a757a8" data-v="4" data-block-id="6a757a8"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-6a757a8-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk--column-flex stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-6a757a8-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns alignfull stk-block-columns stk-block stk-9b456d8" data-block-id="9b456d8"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-9b456d8-column alignfull">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-52c1f35" data-v="4" data-block-id="52c1f35"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-52c1f35-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-52c1f35-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-image stk-block-image stk-block stk-2ff4641 stk-entrance stk-will-enter" data-block-id="2ff4641"><figure class="stk-img-wrapper stk-image--shape-stretch"><img decoding="async" class="stk-img wp-image-10997" src="https://www.myfirstskool.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/curious-thoughtful-and-active-lifelong-learners-1.jpg" width="620" height="338" alt="Curriculum Highlights"></figure></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-a207086" id="title-for-this-block" data-block-id="a207086"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Curious, Thoughtful, and Active Lifelong Learners</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-14c8c86" data-block-id="14c8c86"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">At My First Skool, we do not just focus on teaching academic subjects to our children. We want to impart a love for learning, which is why the acquisition of skills and knowledge is something we strive to make more effective and interesting – through curriculum development, partnerships with leading agencies, or innovative teaching methods.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-button-group stk-block-button-group stk-block stk-ca4d4a1" id="title-for-this-block" data-block-id="ca4d4a1"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-button-group">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-button stk-block-button stk-block stk-6122bcf" data-block-id="6122bcf"><a class="stk-link stk-button stk--hover-effect-darken" href="https://www.myfirstskool.com/our-approach/curriculum/curriculum-highlights/"><span class="has-text-color stk-button__inner-text">See Curriculum Highlights</span></a></div>
</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns alignfull stk-block-columns stk-block stk-33184fc" data-block-id="33184fc"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-33184fc-column alignwide">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-7457384" data-v="4" data-block-id="7457384"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-7457384-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-7457384-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading alignfull stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-33e928d" id="a-holistic-learning-experience-with-petal-sup-sup" data-block-id="33e928d"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">A holistic learning experience with PETAL<sup>©</sup></h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-5d44db5" id="our-core-values-form-the-foundation-of-how-br-we-perform-work-and-conduct-ourselves" data-block-id="5d44db5"><p class="stk-block-text__text">At My First Skool, we empower our children to learn through a pedagogical approach called PETAL<sup>©</sup> – Playing, Exploring, Thinking, and Applying Learning. This approach provides facilitated play experiences that encourage active exploration, critical thinking and making meaningful discoveries.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-cc794fb" data-block-id="cc794fb"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-cc794fb-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-55d8ff1 stk-entrance stk-will-enter" data-v="4" data-block-id="55d8ff1"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-55d8ff1-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-55d8ff1-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-042f7a0 wp-mfs-card-hover-container" data-block-id="042f7a0"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-042f7a0-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-36226c2 front-card" data-v="4" data-block-id="36226c2"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-36226c2-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-36226c2-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-41bebea stk-block-background" data-block-id="41bebea"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-41bebea-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-e0291e1" data-v="4" data-block-id="e0291e1"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-e0291e1-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="has-text-align-center stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-e0291e1-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-a28ae18" id="al" data-block-id="a28ae18"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">P</h2></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns stk-block-columns stk-block stk-591d491" data-block-id="591d491"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-591d491-column">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-d09d935" data-v="4" data-block-id="d09d935"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-d09d935-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-d09d935-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-0ba6c4d" id="span-style-color-var-palette-color-1-dc-6-b-2-f-class-stk-highlight-p-span-laying" data-block-id="0ba6c4d"><h5 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color"><span style="color: var(--theme-palette-color-1, #DC6B2F);" class="stk-highlight">P</span>laying</h5></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-d149746" data-block-id="d149746"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Learning occurs through hands-on games and activities during lessons, and at our Learning Corners.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-3db766a" data-block-id="3db766a"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">Children develop strong listening, speaking, reading, and writing skills when they interact with their peers early in life. We encourage our children to participate in class discussions and provide opportunities for them to gain confidence via show-and-tell sessions with their teachers and peers. The result: confident and effective communicators in life.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-79411c3" data-block-id="79411c3"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Designed for children aged between two months and 4 years, the Early Years Centre (EYC) programme guarantees a Kindergarten 1 placement for a five-year-old child in a nearby partnered MOE kindergarten. My First Skool currently has three EYCs in Punggol.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-b77f8e2" id="frequently-asked-questions" data-block-id="b77f8e2"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-center">Frequently Asked Questions</h2></div>



<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-dc0dfbb stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="dc0dfbb" data-height="133.375">
<summary class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-1399f26 stk--container-small stk-block-accordion__heading" data-v="4" data-block-id="1399f26"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-1399f26-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-1399f26-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon-label stk-block-icon-label stk-block stk-807502f" data-block-id="807502f"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-9f0d206" id="what-are-the-moe-kindergarten-curriculum-hours-what-should-i-do-if-i-require-full-day-care-service" data-block-id="9f0d206"><p class="stk-block-heading__text"><strong>Why is My First Skool providing a preschool service that caters only to children aged 0 to 4 years?</strong></p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-8a0018f" data-block-id="8a0018f"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-8a0018f" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-8-a-0018-f-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-8-a-0018-f-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>
</div></div>
</div></div></summary>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-ad190d1 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="ad190d1"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-ad190d1-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-ad190d1-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-e06001f" data-block-id="e06001f"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">My First Skool (MFS) is partnering with MOE Kindergartens to provide preschool education for children aged between two months and four years. Under this collaboration, MFS operates an EYC to provide infant care and childcare services. Five and six-year-old children will then continue their Kindergarten 1 (K1) and Kindergarten 2 (K2) programme at a partner MOE Kindergarten. This new model will help to increase the number of quality and affordable preschool places in Punggol, so as to support the needs of young families in the area.</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</details>



<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-9ab51e7 stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="9ab51e7" data-height="163.0625">
<summary class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-95a37c7 stk--container-small stk-block-accordion__heading" data-v="4" data-block-id="95a37c7"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-95a37c7-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-95a37c7-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon-label stk-block-icon-label stk-block stk-ef42a2c" data-block-id="ef42a2c"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-9b6daea" id="what-are-the-moe-kindergarten-curriculum-hours-what-should-i-do-if-i-require-full-day-care-service" data-block-id="9b6daea"><p class="stk-block-heading__text"><strong>If I decide not to enrol my child in an MOE Kindergarten, will I be guaranteed a place in other MFS centres which provide K1 and K2 classes?</strong></p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-894ddac" data-block-id="894ddac"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-894ddac" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-894-ddac-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-894-ddac-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>
</div></div>
</div></div></summary>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-75a7572 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="75a7572"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-75a7572-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-75a7572-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-4a3883b" data-block-id="4a3883b"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">You may request to be transferred to other MFS centres. However, successful enrolment will be dependent on the centre’s vacancies.</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</details>



<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-547862e stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="547862e" data-height="133.375">
<summary class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-3153f4b stk--container-small stk-block-accordion__heading" data-v="4" data-block-id="3153f4b"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-3153f4b-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-3153f4b-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon-label stk-block-icon-label stk-block stk-3ea0dad" data-block-id="3ea0dad"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-4e14d87" id="what-are-the-moe-kindergarten-curriculum-hours-what-should-i-do-if-i-require-full-day-care-service" data-block-id="4e14d87"><p class="stk-block-heading__text"><strong>Will my child be guaranteed a space in an MOE Kindergarten when he turns 5?</strong></p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-119aff7" data-block-id="119aff7"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-119aff7" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-119-aff-7-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-119-aff-7-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>
</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-87e371f stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="87e371f"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-87e371f-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-87e371f-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-762f994" data-block-id="762f994"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">All eligible Singaporean children enrolled in our EYC programme’s nursery class will be guaranteed a K1 place in one of our partnered MOE Kindergartens. Your child will be enrolled in the partnered MOE Kindergarten through a pre-admissions phase of the MOE Kindergarten registration exercise, conducted during their nursery year.</p></div>
